\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{"{}Arenas"{}\ are\ fixed\ area's\ of\ OS\ memory\ from\ which\ we\ can\ allocate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{large\ blocks\ (>=\ MI\_ARENA\_MIN\_BLOCK\_SIZE,\ 4MiB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{In\ contrast\ to\ the\ rest\ of\ mimalloc,\ the\ arenas\ are\ shared\ between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{threads\ and\ need\ to\ be\ accessed\ using\ atomic\ operations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{Arenas\ are\ also\ used\ to\ for\ huge\ OS\ page\ (1GiB)\ reservations\ or\ for\ reserving}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{OS\ memory\ upfront\ which\ can\ be\ improve\ performance\ or\ is\ sometimes\ needed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{on\ embedded\ devices.\ We\ can\ also\ employ\ this\ with\ WASI\ or\ \`{}sbrk`\ systems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{to\ reserve\ large\ arenas\ upfront\ and\ be\ able\ to\ reuse\ the\ memory\ more\ effectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ arena\ allocation\ needs\ to\ be\ thread\ safe\ and\ we\ use\ an\ atomic\ bitmap\ to\ allocate.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ }
